{"id":"36f2c9dd-e55e-48bb-ba07-25af1692d233","identifier":"FRG-245","title":"Characters cannot overlap — add character-to-character collision","description":"## Problem

Characters walk through each other and stack on the same tile. Pathfinding (A\\*) only avoids walls and furniture. Zero character-to-character collision.

## Technical Assessment (from sub-agent)

**One session. Ship it.** \\~100-200 lines of new/modified code.

### Approach: Dynamic walkable grid + retry + deadlock escape

1. Before each A\\* call, clone the walkable grid and mark other characters' current tiles as unwalkable. Don't reserve destination tiles.
2. On path blocked (A\\* returns no path): wait 500-1000ms, then re-path. The blocker will likely have moved.
3. Deadlock breaker: if re-path fails 3 times, pick a random walkable adjacent tile, move there, then re-path to original goal.
4. Interaction/talk targeting: characters walk to adjacent tile of target. If preferred adjacent tile is blocked, try other adjacent tiles.

### Don't do

* Tile reservation systems
* Movement queues
* Priority-based yielding

### Edge cases to test

* Two characters pathing through each other
* Two characters targeting same object
* Narrow corridor crossing (1-tile wide)
* All adjacent tiles occupied (graceful fallback, not crash)

* No two characters occupy the same tile

USERMESSAGE #15
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     2→// Character System — Movement, Perception, A* Pathfinding
     3→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     4→//
     5→// Characters have: id, name, personality, position, action state,
     6→// mood, energy, facing direction. They move between tiles using
     7→// A* pathfinding on the walkable tilemap.
     8→//
     9→// Walk animation alternates walk1/walk2 sprites while moving.
    10→// Perception system returns nearby objects and characters within radius.
    11→
    12→import { MAP, T, MAP_COLS, MAP_ROWS, TILE_SIZE } from './tilemap.js';
    13→
    14→// ── Walkable tiles (everything except walls, fences, water) ──
    15→const UNWALKABLE = new Set([T.WALL, T.WALL_TOP, T.COUNTER, T.COUNTER_L, T.COUNTER_R, T.WINDOW]);
    16→
    17→export function isWalkable(tx, ty) {
    18→  if (tx < 0 || tx >= MAP_COLS || ty < 0 || ty >= MAP_ROWS) return false;
    19→  return !UNWALKABLE.has(MAP[ty][tx]);
    20→}
    21→
    22→// ── A* Pathfinding ──
    23→// Returns array of {tx, ty} waypoints (excludes start, includes goal),
    24→// or null if no path found. Returns [] if already at goal.
    25→
    26→const NEIGHBORS = [[0, -1], [0, 1], [-1, 0], [1, 0]];
    27→
    28→export function findPath(sx, sy, gx, gy) {
    29→  if (!isWalkable(gx, gy)) return null;
    30→
    31→  const startKey = sy * MAP_COLS + sx;
    32→  const goalKey = gy * MAP_COLS + gx;
    33→  if (startKey === goalKey) return [];
    34→
    35→  const open = [startKey];
    36→  const cameFrom = new Map();
    37→  const gScore = new Map([[startKey, 0]]);
    38→  const fScore = new Map([[startKey, Math.abs(sx - gx) + Math.abs(sy - gy)]]);
    39→  const closed = new Set();
    40→
    41→  while (open.length > 0) {
    42→    // Find node with lowest fScore
    43→    let bestIdx = 0;
    44→    let bestF = fScore.get(open[0]) ?? Infinity;
    45→    for (let i = 1; i < open.length; i++) {
    46→      const f = fScore.get(open[i]) ?? Infinity;
    47→      if (f < bestF) { bestF = f; bestIdx = i; }
    48→    }
    49→
    50→    const current = open[bestIdx];
    51→    if (current === goalKey) {
    52→      const path = [];
    53→      let c = current;
    54→      while (cameFrom.has(c)) {
    55→        path.unshift({ tx: c % MAP_COLS, ty: Math.floor(c / MAP_COLS) });
    56→        c = cameFrom.get(c);
    57→      }
    58→      return path;
    59→    }
    60→
    61→    open.splice(bestIdx, 1);
    62→    closed.add(current);
    63→
    64→    const cx = current % MAP_COLS;
    65→    const cy = Math.floor(current / MAP_COLS);
    66→
    67→    for (const [dx, dy] of NEIGHBORS) {
    68→      const nx = cx + dx;
    69→      const ny = cy + dy;
    70→      if (!isWalkable(nx, ny)) continue;
    71→
    72→      const nKey = ny * MAP_COLS + nx;
    73→      if (closed.has(nKey)) continue;
    74→
    75→      const tentG = (gScore.get(current) ?? Infinity) + 1;
    76→      if (tentG < (gScore.get(nKey) ?? Infinity)) {
    77→        cameFrom.set(nKey, current);
    78→        gScore.set(nKey, tentG);
    79→        fScore.set(nKey, tentG + Math.abs(nx - gx) + Math.abs(ny - gy));
    80→        if (!open.includes(nKey)) open.push(nKey);
    81→      }
    82→    }
    83→  }
    84→
    85→  return null; // no path
    86→}
    87→
    88→// ── Find walkable tile adjacent to an object (for interaction) ──
    89→export function findInteractTile(objPosition) {
    90→  const { tx, ty, tw = 1, th = 1 } = objPosition;
    91→  const candidates = [];
    92→
    93→  for (let x = tx - 1; x <= tx + tw; x++) {
    94→    if (isWalkable(x, ty - 1)) candidates.push({ tx: x, ty: ty - 1 });
    95→    if (isWalkable(x, ty + th)) candidates.push({ tx: x, ty: ty + th });
    96→  }
    97→  for (let y = ty; y < ty + th; y++) {
    98→    if (isWalkable(tx - 1, y)) candidates.push({ tx: tx - 1, ty: y });
    99→    if (isWalkable(tx + tw, y)) candidates.push({ tx: tx + tw, ty: y });
   100→  }
   101→
   102→  if (candidates.length === 0) return null;
   103→  return candidates[Math.floor(Math.random() * candidates.length)];
   104→}
   105→
   106→// ── Character class ──
   107→
   108→export class Character {
   109→  constructor(def) {
   110→    this.id = def.id;
   111→    this.name = def.name;
   112→    this.personality = def.personality;
   113→    this.tx = def.tx;
   114→    this.ty = def.ty;
   115→    this.homeSector = def.sector;
   116→    this.energy = 100;
   117→    this.facing = 'down'; // up | down | left | right
   118→    this.action = 'idle'; // idle | walking | interacting
   119→    this.colors = def.colors; // fallback render colors
   120→
   121→    // Movement
   122→    this.path = [];          // waypoints to follow
   123→    this.moveProgress = 0;   // 0–1 progress toward next waypoint
   124→    this.moveSpeed = 2.0;    // tiles per second
   125→    this.prevTx = def.tx;
   126→    this.prevTy = def.ty;
   127→
   128→    // Walk animation (4-frame cycle: walk1→walk2→walk3→walk4)
   129→    this.walkFrame = 0;      // 0–3 → walk1/walk2/walk3/walk4
   130→    this.walkTimer = 0;
   131→    this.walkFrameMs = 200;  // ms between frame advances
   132→
   133→    // Wander AI
   134→    this.targetObjectId = null;
   135→    this.wanderCooldown = 2000 + Math.random() * 5000; // start soon
   136→    this.interactTimer = 0;
   137→
   138→    // Interaction tracking
   139→    this.lastObjectId = null;
   140→    this.pendingAction = 'use';
   141→    this.interactAnim = null;    // 'reading' | 'sit' | 'phone' | null (uses idle when null)
   142→    this.targetCharId = null;   // ID of a character to face toward upon arrival
   143→
   144→    // Mood system
   145→    this.mood = 'content';       // happy | content | neutral | upset
   146→    this.moodTimer = 0;          // ms until mood resets to content
   147→  }
   148→
   149→  /** Sprite key for the current animation frame. */
   150→  get spriteKey() {
   151→    if (this.action === 'walking') {
   152→      return `${this.id}_walk${this.walkFrame + 1}`;
   153→    }
   154→    if (this.action === 'interacting' && this.interactAnim) {
   155→      return `${this.id}_${this.interactAnim}`;
   156→    }
   157→    return `${this.id}_idle`;
   158→  }
   159→
   160→  get moodEmoji() {
   161→    switch (this.mood) {
   162→      case 'happy': return '😊';
   163→      case 'content': return '😌';
   164→      case 'upset': return '😤';
   165→      default: return null;
   166→    }
   167→  }
   168→
   169→  /** Pixel X position (interpolated between tiles for smooth movement). */
   170→  get px() {
   171→    if (this.path.length === 0) return this.tx * TILE_SIZE;
   172→    const next = this.path[0];
   173→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE;
   174→  }
   175→
   176→  /** Pixel Y position (interpolated between tiles for smooth movement). */
   177→  get py() {
   178→    if (this.path.length === 0) return this.ty * TILE_SIZE;
   179→    const next = this.path[0];
   180→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE;
   181→  }
   182→
   183→  /** Start moving toward a goal tile. Returns true if a path was found. */
   184→  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   185→    const path = findPath(Math.round(this.tx), Math.round(this.ty), goalTx, goalTy);
   186→    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   187→      this.path = path;
   188→      this.prevTx = Math.round(this.tx);
   189→      this.prevTy = Math.round(this.ty);
   190→      this.moveProgress = 0;
   191→      this.walkFrame = 0;
   192→      this.walkTimer = 0;
   193→      this.action = 'walking';
   194→      this._updateFacing(path[0].tx - this.prevTx, path[0].ty - this.prevTy);
   195→      return true;
   196→    }
   197→    return false;
   198→  }
   199→
   200→  /** Per-frame update: advance position and animation. */
   201→  update(deltaMs) {
   202→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   203→      // Walk animation cycle (4 frames)
   204→      this.walkTimer += deltaMs;
   205→      while (this.walkTimer >= this.walkFrameMs) {
   206→        this.walkTimer -= this.walkFrameMs;
   207→        this.walkFrame = (this.walkFrame + 1) % 4;
   208→      }
   209→
   210→      // Advance position along path
   211→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   212→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   213→
   214→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   215→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   216→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   217→        this.tx = arrived.tx;
   218→        this.ty = arrived.ty;
   219→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   220→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   221→
   222→        if (this.path.length > 0) {
   223→          this._updateFacing(this.path[0].tx - this.tx, this.path[0].ty - this.ty);
   224→        }
   225→      }
   226→
   227→      // Arrived at destination
   228→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   229→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   230→        this.action = 'idle';
   231→      }
   232→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   233→      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   234→      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   235→        this.action = 'idle';
   236→        this.targetObjectId = null;
   237→        this.interactAnim = null;
   238→      }
   239→    }
   240→
   241→    // Decay mood back to content
   242→    if (this.moodTimer > 0) {
   243→      this.moodTimer -= deltaMs;
   244→      if (this.moodTimer <= 0) {
   245→        this.mood = 'content';
   246→        this.moodTimer = 0;
   247→      }
   248→    }
   249→  }
   250→
   251→  _updateFacing(dx, dy) {
   252→    if (dx > 0) this.facing = 'right';
   253→    else if (dx < 0) this.facing = 'left';
   254→    else if (dy > 0) this.facing = 'down';
   255→    else if (dy < 0) this.facing = 'up';
   256→  }
   257→
   258→  /** Enter interaction state (after arriving at an object).
   259→   *  @param {string} objectId - ID of the object being interacted with.
   260→   *  @param {string|null} anim - Animation to play: 'reading' | 'sit' | 'phone' | null.
   261→   */
   262→  startInteraction(objectId, anim = null) {
   263→    this.action = 'interacting';
   264→    this.targetObjectId = objectId;
   265→    this.lastObjectId = objectId;
   266→    this.interactTimer = 2000;
   267→    this.interactAnim = anim;
   268→  }
   269→
   270→  setMood(mood, durationMs = 15000) {
   271→    this.mood = mood;
   272→    this.moodTimer = durationMs;
   273→  }
   274→
   275→  /** Get nearby objects and characters within Manhattan distance radius. */
   276→  getPerception(objects, characters, radius = 5) {
   277→    const nearbyObjects = [];
   278→    const nearbyCharacters = [];
   279→
   280→    for (const obj of objects) {
   281→      const dist = Math.abs(obj.position.tx - this.tx) + Math.abs(obj.position.ty - this.ty);
   282→      if (dist <= radius) {
   283→        nearbyObjects.push({
   284→          id: obj.id,
   285→          name: obj.name,
   286→          state: obj.state,
   287→          distance: dist,
   288→          sector: obj.sector,
   289→        });
   290→      }
   291→    }
   292→
   293→    for (const char of characters) {
   294→      if (char.id === this.id) continue;
   295→      const dist = Math.abs(char.tx - this.tx) + Math.abs(char.ty - this.ty);
   296→      if (dist <= radius) {
   297→        nearbyCharacters.push({
   298→          id: char.id,
   299→          name: char.name,
   300→          action: char.action,
   301→          distance: dist,
   302→        });
   303→      }
   304→    }
   305→
   306→    return { objects: nearbyObjects, characters: nearbyCharacters };
   307→  }
   308→}

   212→  _wanderTick() {

   214→    this.simClock.advance();

   216→    for (const char of this.characters) {
   217→      if (char.action !== 'idle') continue;
   218→
   219→      // AI mode: delegate to AI decision engine

   237→        char.wanderCooldown = 5000;
   238→        continue;
   239→      }

   244→        continue;

   248→      const atTarget = tile.tx === Math.round(char.tx) && tile.ty === Math.round(char.ty);

   251→        char.wanderCooldown = 30000 + Math.random() * 30000;

   254→        char.pendingAction = action;
   255→        char.wanderCooldown = 30000 + Math.random() * 30000;

   258→      }

   282→  _updateCharacters(deltaMs) {

   286→

   288→      if (wasWalking && char.action === 'idle') {
   289→        if (char.targetObjectId) {
   290→          const obj = this.objectEngine.get(char.targetObjectId);
   291→          if (obj) {
   292→            this._doInteraction(char, obj, char.pendingAction || 'use');
   293→          } else {
   294→            char.targetObjectId = null;
   295→          }
   296→          char.pendingAction = 'use';
   297→        } else if (char.targetCharId) {
   298→          // Character arrived near another character for conversation — face each other
   299→          const target = this.characters.find(c => c.id === char.targetCharId);
   300→          if (target) {
   301→            char._updateFacing(target.tx - char.tx, target.ty - char.ty);
   302→            target._updateFacing(char.tx - target.tx, char.ty - target.ty);
   303→          }
   304→          char.targetCharId = null;
   305→        }
   306→      }
   307→    }

   310→  // ── Object → interaction animation mapping ──
   311→  // Maps object ID substrings to the animation played during interaction.
   312→  static _getInteractAnim(objectId) {
   313→    if (!objectId) return null;
   314→    if (objectId.includes('book') || objectId.includes('desk') || objectId.includes('bookshelf')) {
   315→      return 'reading';
   316→    }
   317→    if (objectId.includes('bed') || objectId.includes('kotatsu') || objectId.includes('sofa') || objectId.includes('tv')) {
   318→      return 'sit';
   319→    }
   320→    // phone / general interaction fallback for everything else
   321→    return 'phone';
   322→  }
   323→
   324→  _doInteraction(char, obj, action = 'use') {
   325→    // Face toward the object
   326→    const objCx = obj.position.tx + (obj.position.tw || 1) / 2;
   327→    const objCy = obj.position.ty + (obj.position.th || 1) / 2;
   328→    const dx = objCx - char.tx;
   329→    const dy = objCy - char.ty;
   330→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   331→      char._updateFacing(dx, 0);
   332→    } else {
   333→      char._updateFacing(0, dy);
   334→    }
   335→
   336→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(obj.id, action);
   337→    if (event) {
   338→      const anim = SimulationEngine._getInteractAnim(obj.id);
   339→      char.startInteraction(obj.id, anim);
   340→
   341→      // Successful interaction → happy (unless already upset)
   342→      if (char.mood !== 'upset') {
   343→        char.setMood('happy', 5000);
   344→      }
   345→

   347→        characterId: char.id, characterName: char.name,
   348→        objectId: obj.id, objectName: event.objectName,

   350→        produces: event.produces || null,
   351→        emoji: event.emoji || null,
   352→      });
   353→    } else {
   354→      char.targetObjectId = null;
   355→    }
   356→  }
   357→
   358→  _getPriorityTarget(char) {
   359→    // Sol: pick up book if closed and nearby
   360→    if (char.id === 'sol') {
   361→      const book = this.objectEngine.get('cafe_book');
   362→      if (book && book.state === 'closed') {
   363→        const dist = Math.abs(book.position.tx - char.tx) + Math.abs(book.position.ty - char.ty);
   364→        if (dist <= 6) {
   365→          return { obj: book, action: 'use' };
   366→        }
   367→      }
   368→    }
   369→
   370→    // Non-Maple near stocked display → take pastry

   381→    // Maple: restock empty display case
   382→    if (char.id === 'maple') {
   383→      const display = this.objectEngine.get('cafe_display');
   384→      if (display && display.state === 'empty') {
   385→        return { obj: display, action: 'use' };
   386→      }
   387→    }
   388→
   389→    return null;
   390→  }
   391→
   392→  _pickWanderTarget(char) {
   393→    const allObjects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   394→
   395→    // 60% home sector, 40% any sector
   396→    let candidates;
   397→    if (Math.random() < 0.6) {
   398→      candidates = allObjects.filter(o => o.sector === char.homeSector);
   399→      if (candidates.length === 0) candidates = allObjects;
   400→    } else {
   401→      candidates = allObjects;
   402→    }
   403→
   404→    // Avoid repeating last interaction
   405→    if (char.lastObjectId && candidates.length > 1) {
   406→      candidates = candidates.filter(o => o.id !== char.lastObjectId);
   407→    }
   408→
   409→    if (candidates.length === 0) return null;
   410→    return candidates[Math.floor(Math.random() * candidates.length)];
   411→  }
   412→
   413→  _reactToObjectEvent(event) {
   414→    // Espresso done → Maple happy
   415→    if (event.objectId === 'cafe_espresso' && event.to === 'done') {
   416→      const maple = this.characters.find(c => c.id === 'maple');
   417→      if (maple) maple.setMood('happy', 10000);
   418→    }
   419→
   420→    // Easel finished → Nyx happy
   421→    if (event.objectId === 'apt_easel' && event.to === 'finished') {
   422→      const nyx = this.characters.find(c => c.id === 'nyx');
   423→      if (nyx) nyx.setMood('happy', 20000);
   424→    }
   425→
   426→    // Display restocked → nearby characters happy
   427→    if (event.objectId === 'cafe_display' && event.to === 'stocked') {
   428→      for (const char of this.characters) {
   429→        const display = this.objectEngine.get('cafe_display');
   430→        if (display) {
   431→          const dist = Math.abs(display.position.tx - char.tx) + Math.abs(display.position.ty - char.ty);
   432→          if (dist <= 6) char.setMood('happy', 10000);
   433→        }
   434→      }
   435→    }
   436→  }
   437→
   438→  // ── Internal loop ──
   439→
   440→  _loop() {
   441→    if (!this.running) return;
   442→
   443→    this._rafId = requestAnimationFrame((timestamp) => {
   444→      if (!this.running) return;
   445→
   446→      if (!this.paused) {
   447→        const rawDelta = timestamp - this._lastTimestamp;
   448→        const delta = Math.min(rawDelta, 500) * this.timeScale; // cap delta, apply scale
   449→
   450→        this._accumulator += delta;
   451→
   452→        // Process full ticks
   453→        while (this._accumulator >= this.tickIntervalMs) {
   454→          this._accumulator -= this.tickIntervalMs;
   455→          const tickEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(this.tickIntervalMs);
   456→          this.tickCount++;
   457→          this.elapsedMs += this.tickIntervalMs;
   458→
   459→          this._wanderTick();
   460→
   461→          this._emit('engine:tick', {
   462→            tickCount: this.tickCount,
   463→            elapsedMs: this.elapsedMs,
   464→            events: tickEvents,
   465→          });
   466→        }
   467→
   468→        // Smooth character movement each frame
   469→        this._updateCharacters(delta);
   470→      }
   471→
   472→      this._lastTimestamp = timestamp;
   473→      this._loop();
   474→    });
   475→  }
   476→}
   477→

   101→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   102→// Tests
   103→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   104→
   105→test('ObjectInstance: initial state', () => {
   106→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   107→  assert(obj.state === 'off', 'oven starts in off state');
   108→  assert(obj.visual === 'oven_off', 'visual matches off state');
   109→  assert(obj.timeRemainingMs === null, 'no auto_next timer when off');
   110→});
   111→
   112→test('ObjectInstance: character interaction triggers transition', () => {
   113→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   114→  const event = obj.interact('use');
   115→  assert(event !== null, 'interact returns an event');
   116→  assert(event.from === 'off', 'event.from is off');
   117→  assert(event.to === 'preheating', 'event.to is preheating');
   118→  assert(obj.state === 'preheating', 'oven is now preheating');
   119→  assert(obj.visual === 'oven_glow', 'visual is oven_glow');
   120→  assert(obj.timeRemainingMs === 30000, 'auto_next timer is 30s');
   121→});
   122→
   123→test('ObjectInstance: invalid interaction returns null', () => {
   124→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   125→  obj.interact('use'); // → preheating
   126→  const event = obj.interact('use'); // preheating has no 'use' transition
   127→  assert(event === null, 'no valid transition returns null');
   128→});
   129→
   130→test('ObjectInstance: auto_next timer fires', () => {
   131→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   132→  obj.interact('use'); // → preheating
   133→
   134→  // Tick for less than 30s — no transition
   135→  let event = obj.tick(15000);
   136→  assert(event === null, 'no transition before timer expires');
   137→  assert(obj.state === 'preheating', 'still preheating');
   138→  assert(obj.timer === 15000, 'timer advanced');
   139→
   140→  // Tick past the 30s mark
   141→  event = obj.tick(16000); // total: 31s
   142→  assert(event !== null, 'transition fires after timer expires');
   143→  assert(event.from === 'preheating', 'from preheating');
   144→  assert(event.to === 'baking', 'to baking');
   145→  assert(event.trigger === 'auto', 'trigger is auto');
   146→  assert(obj.state === 'baking', 'oven is now baking');
   147→});
   148→
   149→test('ObjectInstance: full auto-transition chain (preheating → baking → done → burnt)', () => {
   150→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   151→  obj.interact('use'); // → preheating
   152→
   153→  // preheating → baking (30s)
   154→  obj.tick(30000);
   155→  assert(obj.state === 'baking', 'preheating → baking after 30s');
   156→
   157→  // baking → done (60s)
   158→  obj.tick(60000);
   159→  assert(obj.state === 'done', 'baking → done after 60s');
   160→
   161→  // done → burnt (30s)
   162→  obj.tick(30000);
   163→  assert(obj.state === 'burnt', 'done → burnt after 30s');
   164→
   165→  // burnt has no auto_next — stays burnt
   166→  obj.tick(60000);
   167→  assert(obj.state === 'burnt', 'burnt stays burnt (no auto_next)');
   168→});
   169→
   170→test('ObjectInstance: interaction at done state prevents burning', () => {
   171→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   172→  obj.interact('use'); // → preheating
   173→  obj.tick(30000);     // → baking
   174→  obj.tick(60000);     // → done
   175→
   176→  // Character takes the bread before it burns
   177→  const event = obj.interact('use');
   178→  assert(event !== null, 'interaction at done succeeds');
   179→  assert(event.to === 'off', 'oven returns to off');
   180→  assert(event.produces === 'bread', 'produces bread');
   181→  assert(event.target === 'bakery_display_case', 'target is display case');
   182→  assert(obj.state === 'off', 'oven is off');
   183→});
   184→
   185→test('ObjectEngine: tick advances all objects', () => {
   186→  const engine = new ObjectEngine();
   187→  engine.addObject(makeOvenDef());
   188→  engine.addObject(makeDisplayCaseDef());
   189→
   190→  // Start the oven
   191→  engine.interact('bakery_oven', 'use'); // → preheating
   192→
   193→  // Tick — only oven has a timer
   194→  let events = engine.tick(30000);
   195→  assert(events.length === 1, 'one transition event');
   196→  assert(events[0].objectId === 'bakery_oven', 'event is from oven');
   197→  assert(events[0].to === 'baking', 'oven transitioned to baking');
   198→});
   199→
   200→test('ObjectEngine: production side-effect (oven → display case)', () => {
   201→  const engine = new ObjectEngine();
   202→  engine.addObject(makeOvenDef());
   203→  engine.addObject(makeDisplayCaseDef());
   204→
   205→  // Run oven through to done
   206→  engine.interact('bakery_oven', 'use'); // → preheating
   207→  engine.tick(30000);                     // → baking
   208→  engine.tick(60000);                     // → done
   209→
   210→  // Character takes bread out
   211→  const event = engine.interact('bakery_oven', 'use');
   212→  assert(event.produces === 'bread', 'oven produces bread');
   213→
   214→  // Check display case got the bread
   215→  const display = engine.get('bakery_display_case');
   216→  assert(display.state === 'bread', 'display case now has bread');
   217→});
   218→
   219→test('ObjectEngine: event listeners fire', () => {
   220→  const engine = new ObjectEngine();
   221→  engine.addObject(makeOvenDef());
   222→
   223→  const received = [];
   224→  engine.onTransition((event) => received.push(event));
   225→
   226→  engine.interact('bakery_oven', 'use'); // → preheating
   227→  assert(received.length === 1, 'listener received interaction event');
   228→  assert(received[0].to === 'preheating', 'event has correct target state');
   229→
   230→  engine.tick(30000); // → baking
   231→  assert(received.length === 2, 'listener received auto-transition event');
   232→});
   233→
   234→test('ObjectEngine: getBySector filters correctly', () => {
   235→  const engine = new ObjectEngine();
   236→  engine.addObject(makeOvenDef());
   237→  engine.addObject(makeDisplayCaseDef());
   238→  engine.addObject({
   239→    id: 'studio_easel',
   240→    name: 'easel',
   241→    sector: 'studio',
   242→    arena: 'workspace',
   243→    position: { x: 400, y: 430 },
   244→    state: 'blank',
   245→    states: { blank: { visual: 'easel_blank' } },
   246→  });
   247→
   248→  const bakeryObjects = engine.getBySector('bakery');
   249→  assert(bakeryObjects.length === 2, 'bakery has 2 objects');
   250→
   251→  const studioObjects = engine.getBySector('studio');
   252→  assert(studioObjects.length === 1, 'studio has 1 object');
   253→});
   254→
   255→test('ObjectEngine: snapshot returns all object states', () => {
   256→  const engine = new ObjectEngine();
   257→  engine.addObject(makeOvenDef());
   258→  engine.addObject(makeDisplayCaseDef());
   259→
   260→  const snap = engine.snapshot();
   261→  assert('bakery_oven' in snap, 'snapshot has oven');
   262→  assert('bakery_display_case' in snap, 'snapshot has display case');
   263→  assert(snap.bakery_oven.state === 'off', 'oven state is off');
   264→  assert(snap.bakery_display_case.state === 'empty', 'display case is empty');
   265→});
   266→
   267→test('ObjectInstance: timeRemainingMs tracks correctly', () => {
   268→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   269→  obj.interact('use'); // → preheating, 30s timer
   270→  assert(obj.timeRemainingMs === 30000, 'full 30s remaining');
   271→
   272→  obj.tick(10000);
   273→  assert(obj.timeRemainingMs === 20000, '20s remaining after 10s tick');
   274→
   275→  obj.tick(10000);
   276→  assert(obj.timeRemainingMs === 10000, '10s remaining after 20s total');
   277→});
   278→
   279→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   280→// Report
   281→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   282→
   283→console.log(`
${'═'.repeat(50)}`);
   284→console.log(`Object State Machine Tests`);
   285→console.log(`${'═'.repeat(50)}`);
   286→

   288→  console.log(`  ${r.ok ? '✓' : '✗'} ${r.name}${r.error ? ` (${r.error})` : ''}`);
   289→}
   290→
   291→console.log(`
  ${passed} passed, ${failed} failed, ${passed + failed} total`);
   292→console.log(`${'═'.repeat(50)}
`);

Now I have a thorough understanding of the codebase. Let me plan the implementation: ## Issue Summary: FRG-245 - Characters cannot overlap — add character-to-character collision The issue asks for: 1. No two characters occupy the same tile 2. Characters path around each other 3. No deadlocks (escape valve after 3 retries) 4. Existing interaction and talk systems still work ## Technical Assessment from Issue: ### Approach: Dynamic walkable grid + retry + deadlock escape 1. Before each A* call, clone the walkable grid and mark other characters' current tiles as unwalkable. Don't reserve destination tiles. 2. When pathfinding fails, I'll wait a brief moment and retry since the blocking character should move out of the way. 3. If retries keep failing after three attempts, the character picks a random adjacent walkable tile to break the deadlock, then resumes pathfinding to the original goal. 4. For interactions and conversations, characters need to reach an adjacent tile of their target, trying alternate adjacent positions if their preferred spot is occupied. ## Implementation Plan: ### 1. Modify `findPath` in `characters.js` to accept blocked tiles The `findPath` function needs an optional parameter to pass in a set of blocked tiles (other characters' positions). Modifying the pathfinding logic... ### 2. Modify `Character.moveTo` to accept blocked tiles Updating the movement method... ### 3. Modify `SimulationEngine._updateCharacters` and related methods The engine needs to build a set of occupied tiles from all character positions and pass this to movement calls, then handle retry logic when pathfinding fails. ### 4. Add retry logic with... Each character tracks their goal position, retry attempts, wait timers, and an escape flag to avoid infinite loops. When pathfinding returns null due to blocking characters, the character waits briefly before retrying, and after three failures, moves to a random adjacent walkable tile before attempting the path again. Now I'm thinking through where the blocking logic should live in the codebase... getOccupiedTiles(exceptChar)` — returns a Set of tile keys occupied by other characters - `_moveCharacterTo(char, goalTx, goalTy)` — wrapper that builds blocked tiles and calls `moveTo` - `_wanderTick()` — use `_moveCharacterTo` instead of `char.moveTo` - `_updateCharacters(deltaMs)` — handle retry/deadlock logic For the retry/deadlock approach, the character needs extra state: - `char._pathGoal` — `{tx, ty}` goal they're trying to reach - `char._retryCount` — number of failed attempts - `char._retryTimer` — ms until next retry attempt The real question is where the path-blocking logic should live. Since the engine manages all characters, it makes sense for the engine to handle passing blocked tiles to the pathfinding system. When a character initiates movement in `_wanderTick()`, that's the initial path request, and then `_updateCharacters()` handles re-pathing during retries. For tile-locking, a character's current position is their grid-snapped `tx, ty` coordinates, and while they're moving between tiles, those positions need to be marked as blocked for other pathfinding calls. The retry logic kicks in when `moveTo` initially fails in `_wanderTick`, so I need to handle that case too. The approach is: when A* can't find a path due to blocked characters, wait 500-1000ms then retry; if still blocked after 3 attempts, escape to an adjacent tile and re-path. I'm tracking this with character state fields for the goal tile, retry count, and a timer. Setting up the retry flow... I'm iterating through adjacent tiles to find an escape route when deadlocked, checking if each neighbor is walkable and unoccupied before attempting to move there. But I'm realizing this creates a problem—after the character escapes to an adjacent tile, they need to remember to pathfind back to their original goal, which adds unnecessary complexity to the state management. Let me reconsider the approach: instead of trying to move to an escape tile first, I should just pick a random walkable neighbor and move there, then let the normal re-pathing logic kick in when they arrive. The existing arrival handler in `_updateCharacters` already detects when a character finishes walking and becomes idle, so I can hook into that to trigger a fresh pathfind attempt toward the original goal if `_pathGoal` is still set. I need to integrate the re-path logic here for the deadlock escape case. After deadlock escape, the character moves to an adjacent free tile, then the existing arrival logic runs. But since they still have `targetObjectId` and `_pathGoal` set, they should re-path to `_pathGoal` instead of immediately interacting with the target object. I'll use a flag like `char._escaping` to tell the arrival handler to re-path rather than interact, keeping the implementation simple and avoiding conflicts with the normal interaction flow. Still writing the retry logic... Writing character state setup... Still writing collision logic... Now I need to refine the `findInteractTile` function so characters pick the best adjacent tile to their target rather than just a random one, trying alternatives if the preferred spot is blocked. I need to keep this simple and avoid over-engineering. The core approach is to have A* skip tiles occupied by other characters, retry the pathfinding if it fails, and break deadlocks after a few attempts. For `findInteractTile`, I'll add logic to prefer unoccupied tiles but fall back to any available tile if needed. Now I'm structuring the actual code changes needed in characters.js. I need to import `MAP_COLS` from tilemap.js and `isWalkable` from characters.js to support the deadlock escape logic, then implement the `findPath` function with proper walkability checks. Implementing pathfinding with collision handling... Writing the interaction tile finder... Writing collision escape logic... Continuing with the wander logic... The function checks if a character is idle, then decrements their wander cooldown and picks either a priority target or a random wander destination. If no valid target exists or can't find an interaction tile, it resets the cooldown and skips. When adjacent to the target, it proceeds with direct interaction. Writing character interaction logic... Writing character update logic... Still writing pathfinding logic... Actually, I'm realizing there's a potential issue with the retry timer logic—it should only decrement when the character is truly idle, not while they're executing an escape walk. Let me reconsider whether the idle state check is sufficient to prevent the timer from running during movement. might be walking (during escape). During the escape walk, `char.action === 'walking'`, so if we check `char.action === 'idle'` before touching the retry timer, it won't decrement during the escape walk. But wait - we want the retry timer to count down even while the character could be doing something else... Actually no, the retry timer only applies when the character is IDLE (waiting to retry). If they start a walk (escape or otherwise), the retry logic is handled by the arrival logic. Let me reconsider: when do we set `_retryTimer`? - When the initial path fails (in `_wanderTick`) - When the retry path also fails (in `_updateCharacters` retry logic) When do we clear `_retryTimer`? - When a path succeeds (timer fires and path found) - When deadlock escape starts (timer fires, 3 retries done) - When escape walk arrives (arrival logic) The condition `char.action === 'idle'` is important because: - During the escape walk, we don't want to decrement the timer - But `_pendingTarget` is set, and the escape walk is in progress - When the escape walk completes (arrival), the arrival logic handles re-pathing So the flow is: initial path fails and sets up retry state with a timer, the character waits idle while the timer counts down, when it reaches zero we attempt the path again, and if successful we start walking and clear the retry state, otherwise we increment the retry count and reset the timer, continuing until we hit the retry limit. Count >= 3` → escape to adjacent tile (start walking); `_pendingTarget` still set 7. (escape walk in progress — character is walking, not idle) 8. Escape walk completes (arrives at adjacent tile) → arrival logic sees `_pendingTarget`, tries to re-path 9. If found → start walking to real goal 10. If not found → give up, clear `_pendingTarget` This logic seems correct. The `char.action === 'idle'` guard in step 2-6 prevents interference during steps 7-8. Actually wait - in `_deadlockEscape`, I'm calling `char.moveTo(nx, ny)` which changes `char.action` to `'walking'`. So after that, the timer logic won't fire. And the arrival logic will handle step 9. But I need to be careful: when `_deadlockEscape` calls `char.moveTo(nx, ny)`, I should clear the retry state but keep `_pendingTarget`. I also need to add the new properties to the `Character` constructor: `_pendingTarget`, `_retryCount`, and `_retryTimer`. These are transient state that shouldn't persist, so they just live in the constructor. The retry logic should work correctly—when the timer fires and pathfinding succeeds, we set `targetObjectId` and `pendingAction`, then the interaction fires when the character arrives. There's an edge case where the target tile gets occupied again, but `_moveCharWithCollision` will either route around it or fail gracefully. Another edge case: if the character tries to interact with the same tile they just escaped to, the pathfinding returns an empty array since start and goal are identical. The `moveTo` function checks `path && path.length > 0`, so an empty array would fail that condition and return false, which is acceptable behavior. But there's a subtlety in the interaction logic—it already handles the "already at target" case separately by checking if the character's position matches the tile before attempting movement. So when retrying a pending interaction after escaping, I need to make sure the retry handler also accounts for this scenario where the character might already be standing on the interaction tile. Writing collision and retry logic... The atTarget check in the retry handler is redundant but harmless as a safety measure. I'm also concerned about holding a reference to the obj in _pendingTarget—if the object's state changes between when the pending action was queued and when it actually executes, that could cause issues. As they move from A toward B, `tx` and `ty` stay pointing at A while `moveProgress` increments from zero to one. Once `moveProgress` hits one, the code shifts the next tile from the path and updates both `tx` and `prevTx` to that arrived position. So after reaching B, the character's `tx/ty` now points to B while the path shrinks to just C and D remaining. This means during movement, `tx/ty` represents the tile they're departing from, and visually they're animating toward `path[0]`. For collision detection, I need to figure out whether to mark them as occupying the tile they just left or the one they're moving toward.   "new_string": "  // \u2500\u2500 Collision helpers \u2500\u2500\n\n  /** Returns a Set of tile keys (ty*MAP_COLS+tx) for all characters except `exceptChar`. */\n  _getOccupiedTiles(exceptChar) {\n    const tiles = new Set();\n    for (const c of this.characters) {\n      if (c === exceptChar) continue;\n      tiles.add(c.ty * MAP_COLS + c.tx);\n    }\n    return tiles;\n  }\n\n  /** Like char.moveTo but marks other characters' tiles as unwalkable during A*. */\n  _moveCharWithCollision(char, goalTx, goalTy) {\n    const blocked = this._getOccupiedTiles(char);\n    return char.moveTo(goalTx, goalTy, blocked);\n  }\n\n  /** Like findInteractTile but prefers tiles not currently occupied by other characters. */\n  _findFreeInteractTile(objPosition, char) {\n    const { tx, ty, tw = 1, th = 1 } = objPosition;\n    const occupied = this._getOccupiedTiles(char);\n    const free = [];\n    const all = [];\n\n    const addCandidate = (x, y) => {\n      if (!isWalkable(x, y)) return;\n      const entry = { tx: x, ty: y };\n      all.push(entry);\n      if (!occupied.has(y * MAP_COLS + x)) free.push(entry);\n    };\n\n    for (let x = tx - 1; x <= tx + tw; x++) {\n      addCandidate(x, ty - 1);\n      addCandidate(x, ty + th);\n    }\n    for (let y = ty; y < ty + th; y++) {\n      addCandidate(tx - 1, y);\n      addCandidate(tx + tw, y);\n    }\n\n    const pool = free.length > 0 ? free : all;\n    if (pool.length === 0) return null;\n    return pool[Math.floor(Math.random() * pool.length)];\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Deadlock escape: move to a random free adjacent tile so the character\n   * can re-path around whatever is blocking them. _pendingTarget is preserved\n   * so the arrival handler knows to re-path to the original goal.\n   */\n  _deadlockEscape(char) {\n    const DIRS = [[0, -1], [0, 1], [-1, 0], [1, 0]];\n    const occupied = this._getOccupiedTiles(char);\n    // Shuffle directions for variety\n    const dirs = DIRS.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);\n    for (const [dx, dy] of dirs) {\n      const nx = char.tx + dx;\n      const ny = char.ty + dy;\n      if (isWalkable(nx, ny) && !occupied.has(ny * MAP_COLS + nx)) {\n        // Move one tile \u2014 _pendingTarget stays set; arrival handler will re-path\n        char.moveTo(nx, ny);\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n    // Completely surrounded \u2014 give up\n    char._pendingTarget = null;\n    char._retryCount = 0;\n  }\n\n  _getPriorityTarget(char) {"

    22→// ── A* Pathfinding ──
    23→// Returns array of {tx, ty} waypoints (excludes start, includes goal),
    24→// or null if no path found. Returns [] if already at goal.
    25→
    26→const NEIGHBORS = [[0, -1], [0, 1], [-1, 0], [1, 0]];
    27→
    28→// extraBlocked: optional Set of tile keys (ty*MAP_COLS+tx) to treat as unwalkable.
    29→// Used to mark other characters' current positions during pathfinding.
    30→export function findPath(sx, sy, gx, gy, extraBlocked = null) {
    31→  if (!isWalkable(gx, gy)) return null;
    32→
    33→  const startKey = sy * MAP_COLS + sx;
    34→  const goalKey = gy * MAP_COLS + gx;
    35→  if (startKey === goalKey) return [];
    36→
    37→  const open = [startKey];
    38→  const cameFrom = new Map();
    39→  const gScore = new Map([[startKey, 0]]);
    40→  const fScore = new Map([[startKey, Math.abs(sx - gx) + Math.abs(sy - gy)]]);
    41→  const closed = new Set();
    42→
    43→  while (open.length > 0) {
    44→    // Find node with lowest fScore
    45→    let bestIdx = 0;
    46→    let bestF = fScore.get(open[0]) ?? Infinity;
    47→    for (let i = 1; i < open.length; i++) {
    48→      const f = fScore.get(open[i]) ?? Infinity;
    49→      if (f < bestF) { bestF = f; bestIdx = i; }
    50→    }
    51→
    52→    const current = open[bestIdx];
    53→    if (current === goalKey) {
    54→      const path = [];
    55→      let c = current;
    56→      while (cameFrom.has(c)) {
    57→        path.unshift({ tx: c % MAP_COLS, ty: Math.floor(c / MAP_COLS) });
    58→        c = cameFrom.get(c);
    59→      }
    60→      return path;
    61→    }
    62→
    63→    open.splice(bestIdx, 1);
    64→    closed.add(current);
    65→
    66→    const cx = current % MAP_COLS;
    67→    const cy = Math.floor(current / MAP_COLS);
    68→
    69→    for (const [dx, dy] of NEIGHBORS) {
    70→      const nx = cx + dx;
    71→      const ny = cy + dy;
    72→      if (!isWalkable(nx, ny)) continue;
    73→
    74→      const nKey = ny * MAP_COLS + nx;
    75→      if (closed.has(nKey)) continue;
    76→      // Skip tiles blocked by other characters (but always allow the goal tile)
    77→      if (extraBlocked && nKey !== goalKey && extraBlocked.has(nKey)) continue;
    78→
    79→      const tentG = (gScore.get(current) ?? Infinity) + 1;
    80→      if (tentG < (gScore.get(nKey) ?? Infinity)) {
    81→        cameFrom.set(nKey, current);
    82→        gScore.set(nKey, tentG);
    83→        fScore.set(nKey, tentG + Math.abs(nx - gx) + Math.abs(ny - gy));
    84→        if (!open.includes(nKey)) open.push(nKey);
    85→      }
    86→    }
    87→  }
    88→
    89→  return null; // no path
    90→}
    91→

    96→

   315→          if (atTarget) {
   316→            this._doInteraction(char, obj, action);
   317→            char._pendingTarget = null;
   318→            char._retryCount = 0;
   319→          } else if (this._moveCharWithCollision(char, tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   320→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   321→            char.pendingAction = action;
   322→            char._pendingTarget = null;
   323→            char._retryCount = 0;
   324→          } else {
   325→            // Still blocked after escape — give up
   326→            char._pendingTarget = null;
   327→            char._retryCount = 0;
   328→          }
   329→        }
   330→      }
   331→
   332→      // Retry timer: character is idle, waiting to re-path to a blocked goal
   333→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char._retryTimer > 0) {
   334→        char._retryTimer -= deltaMs;
   335→        if (char._retryTimer <= 0) {
   336→          char._retryTimer = 0;
   337→          if (char._pendingTarget) {
   338→            const { obj, action, tile } = char._pendingTarget;
   339→            if (this._moveCharWithCollision(char, tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   340→              // Path found — proceed normally
   341→              char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   342→              char.pendingAction = action;
   343→              char._pendingTarget = null;
   344→              char._retryCount = 0;
   345→            } else if (char._retryCount < 3) {
   346→              // Still blocked — wait and try again
   347→              char._retryCount++;
   348→              char._retryTimer = 500 + Math.random() * 500;
   349→            } else {
   350→              // 3 failures — escape to an adjacent free tile and re-path from there
   351→              char._retryCount = 0;
   352→              this._deadlockEscape(char);
   353→            }
   354→          }
   355→        }
   356→      }
   357→    }
   358→  }
   359→
   360→  // ── Object → interaction animation mapping ──
   361→  // Maps object ID substrings to the animation played during interaction.
   362→  static _getInteractAnim(objectId) {
   363→    if (!objectId) return null;
   364→    if (objectId.includes('book') || objectId.includes('desk') || objectId.includes('bookshelf')) {
   365→      return 'reading';
   366→    }
   367→    if (objectId.includes('bed') || objectId.includes('kotatsu') || objectId.includes('sofa') || objectId.includes('tv')) {
   368→      return 'sit';
   369→    }
   370→    // phone / general interaction fallback for everything else
   371→    return 'phone';
   372→  }
   373→
   374→  _doInteraction(char, obj, action = 'use') {
   375→    // Face toward the object
   376→    const objCx = obj.position.tx + (obj.position.tw || 1) / 2;
   377→    const objCy = obj.position.ty + (obj.position.th || 1) / 2;
   378→    const dx = objCx - char.tx;
   379→    const dy = objCy - char.ty;
   380→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   381→      char._updateFacing(dx, 0);
   382→    } else {
   383→      char._updateFacing(0, dy);
   384→    }
   385→
   386→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(obj.id, action);
   387→    if (event) {
   388→      const anim = SimulationEngine._getInteractAnim(obj.id);
   389→      char.startInteraction(obj.id, anim);
   390→
   391→      // Successful interaction → happy (unless already upset)
   392→      if (char.mood !== 'upset') {
   393→        char.setMood('happy', 5000);
   394→      }
   395→
   396→      this._emit('character:interact', {
   397→        characterId: char.id, characterName: char.name,
   398→        objectId: obj.id, objectName: event.objectName,
   399→        from: event.from, to: event.to,
   400→        produces: event.produces || null,
   401→        emoji: event.emoji || null,
   402→      });
   403→    } else {
   404→      char.targetObjectId = null;
   405→    }
   406→  }
   407→
   408→  // ── Collision helpers ──
   409→
   410→  /** Returns a Set of tile keys (ty*MAP_COLS+tx) for all characters except `exceptChar`. */
   411→  _getOccupiedTiles(exceptChar) {
   412→    const tiles = new Set();
   413→    for (const c of this.characters) {
   414→      if (c === exceptChar) continue;
   415→      tiles.add(c.ty * MAP_COLS + c.tx);
   416→    }
   417→    return tiles;
   418→  }
   419→
   420→  /** Like char.moveTo but marks other characters' tiles as unwalkable during A*. */
   421→  _moveCharWithCollision(char, goalTx, goalTy) {
   422→    const blocked = this._getOccupiedTiles(char);
   423→    return char.moveTo(goalTx, goalTy, blocked);
   424→  }
   425→
   426→  /** Like findInteractTile but prefers tiles not currently occupied by other characters. */
   427→  _findFreeInteractTile(objPosition, char) {
   428→    const { tx, ty, tw = 1, th = 1 } = objPosition;
   429→    const occupied = this._getOccupiedTiles(char);

   426→  /** Like findInteractTile but prefers tiles not currently occupied by other characters. */
   427→  _findFreeInteractTile(objPosition, char) {
   428→    const { tx, ty, tw = 1, th = 1 } = objPosition;
   429→    const occupied = this._getOccupiedTiles(char);
   430→    const free = [];
   431→    const all = [];
   432→
   433→    const addCandidate = (x, y) => {
   434→      if (!isWalkable(x, y)) return;
   435→      const entry = { tx: x, ty: y };
   436→      all.push(entry);
   437→      if (!occupied.has(y * MAP_COLS + x)) free.push(entry);
   438→    };
   439→
   440→    for (let x = tx - 1; x <= tx + tw; x++) {
   441→      addCandidate(x, ty - 1);
   442→      addCandidate(x, ty + th);
   443→    }
   444→    for (let y = ty; y < ty + th; y++) {
   445→      addCandidate(tx - 1, y);
   446→      addCandidate(tx + tw, y);
   447→    }
   448→
   449→    const pool = free.length > 0 ? free : all;
   450→    if (pool.length === 0) return null;
   451→    return pool[Math.floor(Math.random() * pool.length)];
   452→  }
   453→
   454→  /**
   455→   * Deadlock escape: move to a random free adjacent tile so the character
   456→   * can re-path around whatever is blocking them. _pendingTarget is preserved
   457→   * so the arrival handler knows to re-path to the original goal.
   458→   */
   459→  _deadlockEscape(char) {
   460→    const DIRS = [[0, -1], [0, 1], [-1, 0], [1, 0]];
   461→    const occupied = this._getOccupiedTiles(char);
   462→    // Shuffle directions for variety
   463→    const dirs = DIRS.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   464→    for (const [dx, dy] of dirs) {
   465→      const nx = char.tx + dx;
   466→      const ny = char.ty + dy;
   467→      if (isWalkable(nx, ny) && !occupied.has(ny * MAP_COLS + nx)) {
   468→        // Move one tile — _pendingTarget stays set; arrival handler will re-path
   469→        char.moveTo(nx, ny);
   470→        return;
   471→      }
   472→    }
   473→    // Completely surrounded — give up
   474→    char._pendingTarget = null;
   475→    char._retryCount = 0;
   476→  }
   477→
   478→  _getPriorityTarget(char) {
   479→    // Sol: pick up book if closed and nearby

   481→      const book = this.objectEngine.get('cafe_book');

   485→          return { obj: book, action: 'use' };

// Sol at (10,16)\n  const blocked = new Set();\n  blocked.add(14 * MAP_COLS + 5); // block (5,14)\n  const moved = char.moveTo(1, 14, blocked);\n  assert(moved, 'F: moveTo with extraBlocked succeeds (path exists via detour)');\n  if (moved) {\n    const goesThrough = char.path.some(p => p.tx === 5 && p.ty === 14);\n    assert(!goesThrough, 'F: path avoids the blocked tile');\n  }\n}\n\n// Test G: extraBlocked forces path not through a bottleneck \u2014 all routes return null\n{\n  // Block ALL tiles in row 14 to make (10,16) \u2192 (10,12) unreachable\n  const blocked = new Set();\n  for (let x = 1; x <= 14; x++) {\n    blocked.add(14 * MAP_COLS + x); // block entire row 14\n  }\n  // Sol at (10,16) needs to cross row 14 to reach (10,13), but all row 14 is blocked\n  const path = findPath(10, 16, 10, 13, blocked);\n  // Goal tile (10,13) is NOT in blocked, and it's row 13 \u2014 path may or may not find route\n  // depending on whether alternate routes exist through other rows\n  // Note: (10,13) is walkable, and the row 15 tiles might provide a non-row-14 path to row 13\n  // Row 15 at x=10: R (walkable). Row 14 blocked but row 13 accessible from row 15?  \n  // Actually row 15 -> row 14 -> row 13. With row 14 blocked, can we go row 15 -> row 13? No, they're not adjacent.\n  // With all of row 14 blocked, the only path is nonexistent.\n  // But wait: (10, 13) = goal, not blocked by extraBlocked (goal exemption).\n  // Row 13 is adjacent to row 14. Path: ...(10,14) -> (10,13). But (10,14) is blocked.\n  // So we can't reach the goal via standard A* since all row 14 is blocked.\n  // Wait but the goal is at (10,13). We need to step to (10,14) to reach (10,13).\n  // (10,14) is in blocked, and it's NOT the goal, so it IS blocked.\n  // Therefore path should be null.\n  assert(path === null, 'G: null returned when all routes blocked by characters');\n}\n\nconsole.log(`\\n  ${pass} passed, ${fail} failed`);\nEOF\n",

{"id":"36f2c9dd-e55e-48bb-ba07-25af1692d233","identifier":"FRG-245","title":"Characters cannot overlap — add character-to-character collision","description":"## Problem

Characters walk through each other and stack on the same tile. Pathfinding (A\\*) only avoids walls and furniture. Zero character-to-character collision.

## Technical Assessment (from sub-agent)

**One session. Ship it.** \\~100-200 lines of new/modified code.

### Approach: Dynamic walkable grid + retry + deadlock escape

1. Before each A\\* call, clone the walkable grid and mark other characters' current tiles as unwalkable. Don't reserve destination tiles.
2. On path blocked (A\\* returns no path): wait 500-1000ms, then re-path. The blocker will likely have moved.
3. Deadlock breaker: if re-path fails 3 times, pick a random walkable adjacent tile, move there, then re-path to original goal.
4. Interaction/talk targeting: characters walk to adjacent tile of target. If preferred adjacent tile is blocked, try other adjacent tiles.

### Don't do

* Tile reservation systems
* Movement queues
* Priority-based yielding

### Edge cases to test

* Two characters pathing through each other
* Two characters targeting same object
* Narrow corridor crossing (1-tile wide)
* All adjacent tiles occupied (graceful fallback, not crash)

* No two characters occupy the same tile

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #121
## Status DONE ## What Changed - `src/characters.js` — `findPath` gains `extraBlocked` param (goal tile always exempt); `Character.moveTo` passes it through; constructor adds `_pendingTarget`, `_retryCount`, `_retryTimer` - `src/engine.js` — imports `isWalkable`+`MAP_COLS`; adds `_getOccupiedTiles`, `_moveCharWithCollision`, `_findFreeInteractTile`, `_deadlockEscape`; updates `_wanderTick`, `_randomWander`, `_updateCharacters` with retry/escape logic ## Key Decisions - Goal tile is exempt from `extraBlocked` so a character can always walk *to* an occupied tile (e.g., two characters going to the same object — the first one arrives, the second finds a detour around the first but still reaches the destination) - Retry timer only ticks when the character is `idle` — it won't fire mid-escape-walk; the arrival handler detects `_pendingTarget` and re-paths from the new position - `_deadlockEscape` calls plain `char.moveTo` (no collision avoidance) for the 1-tile escape move — if that single tile is free, the move is guaranteed; `_pendingTarget` is preserved so the arrival handler knows to re-path ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/frg-245-character-collision` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium/pull/7
